The stoners steak is a little too much and will fall apart before the half to me not ‚Äúsouth‚Äù enough to not just be an everything steak sandwich. The works is my go to for cheesesteak, because why not?

< review>
We have been dine in only customers for years. Due to the new safer at home restrictions, we have been cooking at home. Tonight, we needed a break. We ordered through their website, and our food was ready in 25 minutes. It was even better than the last time we dined in. My chicken wrap was moist, and the salad was super fresh. The gyro wrap was full of tender lamb and the mixed kebabs were perfectly cooked. The fries and rice were perfect too. Everything was packaged nicely and as always the service was friendly. I highly recommend this local spot.</review>

Had the debate with my wife over street pupusas for 1.50 or molcajete for 3-3.50 per pupusa.

I told her 1.50 for an inconsistent flavors and a small sized pupusa with mediocre ingredients on the street and potentially have a " none enjoyable" dinner or go to this restaurant and have a somewhat premium Salvadorean pupusa that you will 100% enjoy at a slightly higher cost.

Guess what the answer was..

Oh and get Get large sides of condiments for the pupusas it goes a long way.

This place has great Salvadorian food. I've ordered Pupusas here a few times and they're pretty tasty. The one thing about them is they make them to order, so expect your food to be ready in 40-45 minutes after you call. I have never dined in, just picked up takeout. My last order had bean and cheese pupusas, regular cheese, and  Carne Asasa fries, which were really robust and tasty!

If you have time to wait and want some good pupusas, I'd recommend. Parking is street parking and it's right on Temple so it can be busy, but if you're just grabbing food it's pretty simple.< /review>

<name>Ayisha Gabri</name>< Review>
My wife and I have always been on the search for good and authentic Mexican food since we moved from California in 1978. This place serves authentic street food!
I had menudo and it was the best I have had outside of Mexico and the Southwest. I also had an outstanding cheese and jalapeno tamale. My wife had a chile relleno which is the best she has had in the East.
The chips are not as fresh as I would like  but the salsas are outstanding.
We ordered two burritos to go. Wow. The spicy pork is outstanding. The Chorizo is equally as good.
This is a classic hole in the wall restaurant. It is not a place for a first date but it is the kind of place where you know you will get good food. It is not fancy. The services is nice.
The prices are incredible when you look at the quality of the food.
I rank it on equal par with Rincon and Los Portales.
Los Molcajetes makes this ex-Californian very happy</Review>
